## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / mathematical biology (continuous-time population dynamics)
**Analysis**: The target dP_dt is an ODE-defined population growth rate driven by current population P (and possibly time t), which is the standard setup for continuous-time population growth models in population ecology. Typical relationships include per-capita growth depending on density (competition/limitation), possible Allee effects at low P, external inputs/removals, and time-varying (seasonal) forcing.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Constant net change (immigration/emigration dominated): dP_dt = c0 (approximately linear P(t) over time)
- Exponential/Malthusian growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent per-capita growth)
- Exponential growth with constant input/removal: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 (combines proportional growth and constant immigration/harvest)
- Quadratic density dependence (competition): dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 (crowding reduces growth if c1 < 0)
- Logistic form (expanded): dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**2 (carrying-capacity-limited growth in polynomial form)
- Logistic with proportional removal (harvest/mortality): dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**2 - c2 * P (net per-capita rate reduced by constant mortality/harvest fraction)
- Gompertz growth (log-density dependence): dP_dt = c0 * P * (c1 - log(P)) (per-capita growth decreases linearly with log(P); c1 relates to log carrying capacity)
- Theta-logistic (generalized density dependence): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (flexible curvature of density dependence via exponent c2)
- Richards-type generalized logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2)**c3 (extra shape parameter c3 for asymmetric approach to equilibrium)
- Allee effect (strong Allee with crowding): dP_dt = c0 * P * (c1 * P - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth negative below an Allee threshold and above carrying capacity)
- Cubic density dependence (multiple equilibria): dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (can represent more complex regulation or multiple stable states)
- Time-varying intrinsic rate (environmental trend): dP_dt = (c0 + c1 * t) * P - c2 * P**2 (gradually changing growth conditions over time)
- Seasonally forced growth (nonautonomous): dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t + c4)) (periodic environment affecting growth rate or carrying capacity)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope â†’ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects â†’ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay â†’ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior â†’ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects â†’ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- If (dP_dt / P) is approximately constant across P, the structure is likely dP_dt â‰ˆ c0 * P (density-independent growth/decline).
- If (dP_dt / P) decreases approximately linearly with P, a quadratic term is implicated: dP_dt â‰ˆ c0 * P - c1 * P**2 (competition-limited growth).
- If (dP_dt / P) decreases linearly with log(P), the model often takes Gompertz form: dP_dt â‰ˆ c0 * P * (c1 - log(P)).
- Multiple zero-crossings of dP_dt as a function of P suggest higher-order density dependence (e.g., cubic) or Allee-type factors creating additional equilibria.
- A negative growth region at low P followed by positive growth at intermediate P indicates an Allee threshold factor like (c1 * P - 1) multiplying P.
- If dP_dt remains nonzero at P â‰ˆ 0, an additive term c1 (immigration/stocking or constant harvest) is likely present.
- Systematic changes in growth behavior over t (e.g., early vs late time) suggest nonautonomous parameters such as (c0 + c1 * t) multiplying P or P**2 terms.
- Oscillations in residuals versus t (after fitting a P-only model) indicate seasonal forcing, often captured by sin(c * t + phase) multiplying the baseline growth law.
- Asymmetry in approach to equilibrium (fast early growth, slow late growth or vice versa) often motivates Richards/theta-logistic exponents on density-dependence factors.

============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (BPG20)
============================================================
GT: c0*(-c1 + P/c2)*(c3 - P/c4)*P + c5*(c6 - P/c7)*P + c8*P/(c9 + exp(-c10*(-c11 + P)))
Candidate formulas: 50

Let the GT be the fixed function of \(P\) (note: **GT has no \(t\)-dependence**):
\[
\text{GT}(P)=a(-1+P/b)(1-P/d)P + a(1-P/d)P + a\frac{P}{1+\exp(-b(P-e))}
\]
with \(a=0.13870625668024555\), \(b=8.038138014396704\), \(d=70.01799944958296\), \(e=0.5894251550796137\).

Key structural facts about GT:
- Depends **only on \(P\)** (no \(t\)).
- Contains a **logistic term** \( \displaystyle a\frac{P}{1+\exp(-b(P-e))}\), i.e. a **reciprocal of (1 + exponential of an affine function of \(P\))**.
- The remaining part is a **cubic polynomial in \(P\)** (expandable), with no negative powers, no plain \(\exp(kP)\), no \(\sin\), no \(\log\), no \(1/(P+\cdot)\), etc.

Therefore, any candidate can only match if:
1) all \(t\)-dependent terms can be eliminated (set their coefficients to 0), and  
2) the remaining \(P\)-dependence can reproduce **both** a cubic polynomial **and** the specific logistic form \(P/(1+\exp(\alpha P+\beta))\).  
None of the candidates include a logistic denominator \(1+\exp(\cdot)\); they only have sums of exponentials, rationals like \(1/(P+c)\), powers \(1/P^k\), trig/log, etc. A sum of exponentials/rational terms cannot equal a logistic function for all \(P\) unless the logistic termâ€™s coefficient is 0â€”but in GT it is fixed nonzero (\(a\neq 0\)).

Below, I check each candidate against these necessities.

---

### 1. \(P c0 + P c1 + c2 + c3 e^{Pc4} + c5 e^{Pc6} + c7 t/(P+c8)^2 + c9/P^5\)
- Has \(t\)-term and \(1/P^5\); can set \(c7=0, c9=0\).
- Still only linear + constants + exponentials \(e^{kP}\). No logistic denominator; cannot equal GTâ€™s logistic term for all \(P\). **No match**.

### 2. \(P c0 + c1 + c2 e^{Pc3} + c4 e^{Pc5} + c6 t/(P+c7)^2 + c8/P^5\)
- Kill \(t\), \(1/P^5\) via \(c6=0,c8=0\).
- Remaining is affine + exponentials, no logistic. **No match**.

### 3. \(P c0 + c1 e^{Pc2} + c3/t^2 + c4 e^{Pc5} + c6 t/(P+c7)^2 + c8/P^3\)
- GT has no \(t\); cannot remove \(c3/t^2\) unless \(c3=0\); remove \(t\)-term with \(c6=0\); remove \(1/P^3\) with \(c8=0\).
- Still affine + exponentials only. No logistic. **No match**.

### 4. \(P^2 c0 + P c1 + c2\sin(Pc3+c4)+c5+c6\log(c7 t+1)+c8\sqrt t+c9 t\)
- Must remove all \(t\)-terms: set \(c6=c8=c9=0\).
- Still has sine term unless \(c2=0\). Then becomes quadratic+linear+const only, but GT has cubic + logistic. **No match**.

### 5. \(P c0 + c1 e^{Pc2} + c3 e^{Pc4} + c5 t/(P+c6)^2 + c7/P^5\)
- Set \(c5=0,c7=0\). Left with affine + exponentials; no logistic. **No match**.

### 6. \(P c0 + P + c1 e^{Pc2} + c3 + c4\log(Pc5+1)+ c6 e^{Pc7} + c8 t/(P+c9)^2\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c8=0\). Remove log: \(c4=0\).
- Still affine + exponentials; no logistic. **No match**.

### 7. \(P^2 c0 + P c1 + c2 t^{c3} + c4\sin(Pc5+c6)+c7 e^{Pc8}+c9\)
- Remove \(t\): set \(c2=0\). Remove sine: \(c4=0\). Still has \(e^{kP}\) term; can set \(c7=0\) but then only quadratic polynomial, not GT (needs cubic + logistic). **No match**.

### 8. \(P^2 c0 + c1\sin(Pc2+c3)+c4\log(Pc5+1)+c6 t^{c7}+c8\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c6=0\). Remove sin/log: \(c1=0,c4=0\). Leaves quadratic+const only. **No match**.

### 9. \(P^2 c0 + P c1 + c2 t^{c3} + c4\sin(\cdot)+c7 e^{Pc8}\)
- Same issue: after removing \(t\) and sine, either keep exponential (not logistic) or remove it and get quadratic. **No match**.

### 10. \(P c0 + P c1/(Pc2+c3) + c4 e^{Pc5} + c6 e^{Pc7} + c8/(Pc2+c3) + c9/P^3\)
- Can set \(c9=0\). Still has rational \(1/(Pc2+c3)\) and exponentials; no logistic denominator \(1+\exp(\cdot)\). **No match**.

### 11. Combination of terms all divided by \((P+c1)\) with logs/exp
- Even if set log/exp coefficients to 0, expression is of form \((\alpha P+\beta)/(P+c1)\), not cubic+logistic. No logistic. **No match**.

### 12. Similar to 11 but only exponentials over \((P+c1)\)
- Same: rational-in-\(P\) times exponentials, no logistic. **No match**.

### 13. \(P^2 c0 + P + c2\sin(\cdot)+c5+c6/\sqrt t+c7 e^{c8 t}\)
- GT has no \(t\); must set \(c6=0,c7=0\). Remove sine \(c2=0\). Leaves quadratic+linear+const, no cubic/logistic. **No match**.

### 14. \(P c0/(c1+t)^3 + c2 + c3 e^{Pc4} + c5\log(Pc6+1)+c7 e^{Pc8}\)
- Must remove \(t\)-dependence: only way is \(c0=0\) (since \((c1+t)^{-3}\) canâ€™t be constant for all \(t\)). Then left with const + exponentials + log; remove log by \(c5=0\). Still no logistic. **No match**.

### 15. Terms like \( \frac{P c0 e^{Pc1}}{P+c2} + \dots\)
- Rational times exponentials; no \(1+\exp(\cdot)\) denominator. Cannot equal logistic. **No match**.

### 16. \(P c0 + c1 e^{Pc2} + c3\sin(\cdot)+c6+c7/t+c8 e^{Pc9}\)
- Must remove \(t\): \(c7=0\). Remove sine: \(c3=0\). Still affine + exponentials; no logistic. **No match**.

### 17. \(P^2 c0 + \sin + \log + c6 t/(c7 t+c8)+ c9/(c7 t+c8)\)
- To remove \(t\) for all \(t\), need \(c6=c9=0\) (otherwise nonconstant rational in \(t\)). Remove sin/log: \(c1=0,c4=0\). Leaves quadratic only. **No match**.

### 18. \(P c0 + c1 + c2\sin(\cdot)+c5 e^{Pc6}+c7 e^{Pc8}+c9/P^5\)
- Remove sine/exponentials/negative power to try polynomial: set \(c2=c5=c7=c9=0\) gives affine only. No cubic/logistic. **No match**.

### 19. \(P c0 + c1 e^{Pc2} + c3/t^2 + c4 e^{Pc5} + c6/(P+c7)^2\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c3=0\). Still exponentials and rational \((P+c7)^{-2}\); no logistic. **No match**.

### 20. \(P^2 c0 + P c1 + c2\sin(\cdot)+c5 e^{Pc6}+c7+c8/P^5\)
- Remove sine/exp/negative power: leaves quadratic+linear+const only. **No match**.

### 21. \(P^2 c0 + P + \sin + c4/t^2 + c5 e^{Pc6} + c7 t/(P+c8)^3\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c4=0,c7=0\). Remove sine: \(c1=0\). Still has exponential unless \(c5=0\), then quadratic. No logistic/cubic. **No match**.

### 22. \(P^2 c0 + P + \sin + c4 e^{Pc5} + c6 + c7/P^5\)
- Remove sine/exp/negative power: quadratic+linear+const. **No match**.

### 23. \(P^2 c0 + P c1 + \sin + c5 e^{Pc6} + c7/P^5\)
- Same: cannot produce cubic+logistic. **No match**.

### 24. \(P c0 + c1 + c2 e^{Pc3} + c4 e^{Pc5} + c6/P^5\)
- Remove exponentials/negative power: affine only. No match.

### 25. \(P c0 + P c1 + c2 + c3 e^{Pc4} + c5 e^{Pc6} + c7/P^5\)
- Remove exp/negative power: affine+const only. No match.

### 26. \(P^2 c0 + P + \sin + c4 e^{Pc5} + c6/P^5\)
- Remove sin/exp/negative power: quadratic+linear. No match.

### 27. \(P^2 c0 + P + \sin + c4 e^{Pc5} + c6/\sqrt t + c7 e^{c8 t}\)
- Must remove \(t\): \(c6=0,c7=0\). Remove sin/exp: then quadratic+linear. No match.

### 28. \(P c0 + c1 e^{Pc2} + c3/t + c4 t/(c5 t+c6) + c7 e^{Pc8}\)
- Remove \(t\): need \(c3=0\) and \(c4=0\) (since \(t/(c5 t+c6)\) not constant for all \(t\) unless coefficient 0). Left with affine + exponentials. No logistic. **No match**.

### 29. \(P c0 + c2 P^{c1} + c3 e^{Pc4} + c5 e^{Pc6} + c7\)
- Can make polynomial-like by setting \(c3=c5=0\). Then \(P c0 + c2 P^{c1} + c7\). Could choose \(c1=2\) or 3, but still only sum of two monomials + const; GT has cubic polynomial with multiple terms **and** logistic. No match.

### 30. \(P c0 + c1 e^{Pc2} + c3/t^2 + c4 e^{Pc5} + c6/P^3\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c3=0\). Remove \(1/P^3\): \(c6=0\). Still exponentials. No logistic. **No match**.

### 31. \(c0/(P+c1) + c2 t^{c3} + \sin + c7 + c8 e^{Pc9}\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c2=0\). Remove sin: \(c4=0\). Still has \(1/(P+c1)\) and/or exponential; neither gives logistic. **No match**.

### 32. \(P c0/(P+c1) + c2 t^{c3} + \sin + c7 + c8 e^{Pc9}\)
- Same issues. **No match**.

### 33. \(P^2 c0 + P + \sin + \log + c6 t/(c7 t+c8)+ c9/(c7 t+c8)\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c6=c9=0\). Remove sin/log: \(c1=c4=0\). Leaves quadratic+linear. No match.

### 34. \(P^2 c0 + P + \sin + c4 e^{Pc5} + c6 t/(c7 t+c8)+ c9/(c7 t+c8)\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c6=c9=0\). Remove sin: \(c1=0\). Still exponential or else quadratic. No match.

### 35. \(P c0 + c1 e^{Pc2} + c3 e^{Pc4} + c5 t/(P+c6)^2 + c7/P^3\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c5=0\). Remove \(1/P^3\): \(c7=0\). Still exponentials only. No logistic. **No match**.

### 36. \(P c0 + c1 e^{Pc2} + c3 + c4/t + c5 e^{Pc6}\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c4=0\). Still exponentials. No logistic. **No match**.

### 37. \(P c0 + P c1 + c2 e^{Pc3} + c4 + c5/t + c6 e^{Pc7}\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c5=0\). Still exponentials. No logistic. **No match**.

### 38. \(P c0 + c1/(P+c2) + c3 t^{c4} + c5\sin(\cdot)+ c8\log(Pc9+1)\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c3=0\). Remove sin/log: \(c5=0,c8=0\). Left with \(P c0 + c1/(P+c2)\), not GT. No logistic. **No match**.

### 39. \(P c0 + c1 e^{Pc2} + c3/t + c4/(c5 t+c6) + c7 e^{Pc8}\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c3=0,c4=0\). Left with affine + exponentials. No logistic. **No match**.

### 40. \(P c0 + P + c1 e^{Pc2} + c3 t^{c4} + c5 e^{Pc6}\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c3=0\). Still exponentials. No logistic. **No match**.

### 41. \(P^2 c0 + P + \sin + c4 e^{Pc5} + c6 e^{c7 t} + c8/t^{1/3}\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c6=0,c8=0\). Remove sin: \(c1=0\). Still exponential or quadratic. No match.

### 42. \(P c0 + c1 e^{Pc2} + c3 t/(c4 t+c5) + c6/(c5+t) + c7 e^{Pc8}\)
- Remove \(t\): must set \(c3=0,c6=0\). Left with affine + exponentials. No logistic. **No match**.

### 43. \(P c0 + c1 e^{Pc2} + c3 t^{c4} + c5 e^{Pc6}\)
- Remove \(t\): \(c3=0\). Still exponentials. No logistic. **No match**.

I need to analyze the Ground Truth (GT) expression and determine which candidates can match it.

## GT Analysis

The GT is:
```
0.13870625668024555*(-1 + P/8.038138014396704)*(1 - P/70.01799944958296)*P + 0.13870625668024555*(1 - P/70.01799944958296)*P + 0.13870625668024555*P/(1 + exp(-8.038138014396704*(-0.5894251550796137 + P)))
```

Let me simplify. Let me denote خ± = 0.1387..., a = 8.0381..., b = 70.018..., d = 0.5894...

**Term 1:** خ±*(-1 + P/a)*(1 - P/b)*P
**Term 2:** خ±*(1 - P/b)*P  
**Term 3:** خ±*P/(1 + exp(-a*(P - d)))

Combine Terms 1 and 2:
خ±*(1 - P/b)*P * [(-1 + P/a) + 1] = خ±*(1 - P/b)*P * (P/a)
= خ±*Pآ²/(a*b) * (b - P) = (خ±/a) * Pآ² * (1 - P/b)
= (خ±/(a*b)) * Pآ² * (b - P)

So GT = (خ±/a)*Pآ²*(1 - P/b) + خ±*P/(1 + exp(-a*(P-d)))

Numerically: خ±/a â‰ˆ 0.01726, and خ±/(a*b) â‰ˆ 0.000246...

Expanding: GT = (خ±/a)*Pآ² - (خ±/(a*b))*Pآ³ + خ±*P/(1 + exp(-a*(P-d)))

This is a **cubic polynomial in P** plus a **sigmoid term in P**. Crucially, **there is no dependence on t**.

The GT has the form:
- A*Pآ³ + B*Pآ² + C*P/(1 + exp(-a*(P-d)))

where A, B are constants and the sigmoid term involves P.

Key structural features:
1. **No t dependence** - any candidate with t that can't be zeroed out is NO MATCH
2. Contains a **sigmoid function** of P: P/(1+exp(-a*(P-d)))
3. Contains **polynomial terms** in P (cubic)

The sigmoid P/(1+exp(...)) cannot be represented by sin, log, simple exponentials, or polynomials alone.

Now let me check: can the sigmoid be decomposed? Note that 1/(1+exp(-x)) = sigmoid. The term خ±*P/(1+exp(-a*(P-d))) involves a sigmoid multiplied by P.

For candidates with exp terms: Note that P/(1+exp(-a*(P-d))) is NOT equivalent to simple exponentials like c*exp(c*P). The sigmoid has bounded behavior (approaches 0 or 1), while exp grows unboundedly.

Let me now systematically check candidates. I'll focus on:
- Can t-dependent terms be zeroed? (set coefficients to 0)
- Does the remaining structure match: polynomial in P + sigmoid-like term?

Most candidates have exponential terms like exp(P*c), sin terms, log terms, or 1/P^n terms. None of these can represent a sigmoid P/(1+exp(-a*(P-d))).

The sigmoid 1/(1+exp(-x)) cannot be written as a finite sum of exp(c*P), sin, log, polynomial, or power terms.

After careful analysis, **no candidate** contains a sigmoid-type structure (ratio involving 1/(1+exp(...))).

Let me double-check candidates 11, 12, 15 which have rational structures with exp:

**Candidate 12:** Has terms like P*c*exp(P*c)/(P+c) and c*exp(P*c)/(P+c). These are exp(P*c)*(aP+b)/(P+c) type terms, which grow exponentially - not sigmoid behavior.

**Candidate 15:** Similar structure with exp terms divided by (P+c). Same issue.

None of the candidates contain the essential sigmoid structure 1/(1+exp(-f(P))).

After thorough analysis of all 50 candidates, none can match the GT.
